# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="2f722-102">.NET Framework 中過時的成員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2f722-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2f722-103">本文中的表格列出 .NET Framework 4.5 和更新版本中依組件分組的已淘汰類型成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2f722-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2f722-104">請使用下列連結，查看每個組件中過時的成員和建議的替代做法清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2f722-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2f722-105">本文不會列出過時的類型成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2f722-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2f722-106">如需過時的型別清單，請參閱[已淘汰類型](obsolete-types.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2f722-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

<a name="SystemMembers"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-members-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="2f722-140">系統組件中過時的成員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2f722-140">Obsolete Members in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="2f722-141">下表列出系統組件中過時的成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2f722-141">The following tables list the obsolete members in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2f722-142">這些組件是用於以 .NET Framework 為目標的一般用途應用程式開發。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2f722-142">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="2f722-1142">組件︰IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2f722-1142">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>
